                  <foreign lang="ar">يَضْحَى عِجَانُهُ</foreign> i. e. [<hi rend="ital">It is approved as a quality of the horse</hi>] <hi rend="ital">that his</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عجان</foreign> [q. v., a word variously expl.,] <hi rend="ital">appear.</hi> (S, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ضَحِيَتِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">اللّيْلَةُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The night was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, cloudless.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ضَحِىَ الفَرَسَ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The horse was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, white.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ظِلُّهُ ضَحَا</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">He died:</hi> (K, TA:) it [properly] means <hi rend="ital">his shade,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">shadow, became sun:</hi> and when a man's shade, or shadow, becomes sun, he himself becomes nought. (IAmb, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">ضَحَا</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">ضَحِىَ</foreign>, aor. of each <foreign lang="ar">يَضْحَى</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">ضَحْوٌ</foreign>, (K, TA,) or, accord. to the M, <foreign lang="ar">ضُحُوٌّ</foreign>, (TA,) and <foreign lang="ar">ضُحِىٌّ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">He,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, was smitten by the sun;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the sun came,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">fell, upon him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it:</hi> (K, TA:) or <foreign lang="ar">ضَحِىَ</foreign>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَضْحَى</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">ضَحًا</foreign>; and <foreign lang="ar">ضَحَا</foreign>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَضْحُو</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">ضَحْوٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">ضُحُوٌّ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">he,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, was smitten by the heat of the sun.</hi> (Ham p. 625.)                   <foreign lang="ar">أَشْهَبُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Of a colour in which whiteness predominates over blackness;</hi> &amp;c.]: fem. <foreign lang="ar">ضَحْيَآءُ</foreign>: (S, K:) or <foreign lang="ar">الضَّحْيَآءُ</foreign> was, (K,) or was also, (S, and so afterwards in the K,) the name of a certain mare, belonging to 'Amr Ibn-'Ámir (S, K) Ibn-Rabee'ah. (S.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">لَيْلَةٌ ضَحْيَآءُ</foreign>, (S, K,) and <foreign lang="ar">ضَحْيَا</foreign> with the short <foreign lang="ar">ا</foreign>, both mentioned by ISd, (TA,) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n25630-1" target="إِضْحِيَانَةٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, (S, K,) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n25630-2" target="إِضْحِيَةٌ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n25631"/></foreign> accord. to the K, but [SM says] I have not found any mention of this last, [meaning except in the K,] and probably the right word is   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n25630-3" target="إِضحِيَانٌ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, as in the books of strange words together with <foreign lang="ar">إِضْحِيَانَةٌ</foreign>, and accord. to the “ Irtisháf ed-Darab ” of AHei one says [also]   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n25630-4" target="أَضْحِيَانٌ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> with fet-h, (TA,) <hi rend="ital">A bright night,</hi> (S, K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">in which are no clouds:</hi> (S, TA:) and in like manner,   
      <foreign lang="ar">يَوْمٌ <ref cref="n25630-5" target="إِضْحِيَانٌ" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n25632"/></foreign>, in the K, erroneously, <foreign lang="ar">ضَحْيَاةٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">a bright day, in which are no clouds,</hi> as in the M; or <hi rend="ital">bright with the brightness of the</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">ضُحَى</foreign>, accord. to Er-Rághib; or [simply] <hi rend="ital">bright,</hi> and so

      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n25630-7" target="إِضْحِيَانٌ" n="7" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n25632"/></foreign>, and to a lamp, or its lighted wick. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">اِمْرَأَةٌ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">ضَحْيَآءُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">A woman whose hair of her</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عَانَة</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">will not grow forth;</hi> (K, TA;) as though her <foreign lang="ar">عانة</foreign>, being bare of hair, had no shade upon it. (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">مَا أَدْرِى أَىُّ الضَّحْيَآءِ هُوَ</foreign> is a saying mentioned by Az in art. <foreign lang="ar">طهى</foreign> as meaning <hi rend="ital">I know not what one of mankind,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">of the people, he is.</hi> (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="3">-A3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَضْحًى</foreign> [a coll. gen. n., of which the n. un. is <foreign lang="ar">أَضْحَاةٌ</foreign>]: see <foreign lang="ar">أُضْحِيَّةٌ</foreign>. Hence, <foreign lang="ar">يَوْمُ الأَضْحَى</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">The day of the victims;</hi> which is the tenth of Dhu-l- Hijjeh]; (S, Mgh, K, * TA;) so says Yaakoob; (TA;) or <foreign lang="ar">عِيدُ الأَضْحَى</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">the festival of the victims</hi>]: (Msb:) and by <foreign lang="ar">الأَضْحَى</foreign> when it is made masc. is meant that day.
